<strong>Linear Regression</strong> indicator (LINEARREG) calculates the linear regression line for a given set of data points, representing the best-fit line that minimizes the distance between the data points and the line. It helps to identify the overall trend direction.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="linearreg-angle" tabindex="-1">linearreg_angle <a class="header-anchor" href="#linearreg-angle" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;linearreg\_angle&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">linearreg_angle(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Linear Regression Angle</strong> (LINEARREG_ANGLE) measures the angle of the linear regression line. It quantifies the slope or steepness of the trend.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 <strong>Linear Regression Slope</strong> is helps to identify potential trends in price movements by analyzing the slope of a linear regression line fitted to past price data. A positive slope suggests an uptrend, while a negative slope suggests a downtrend. The slope&#39;s magnitude indicates the strength of the trend.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="lrsi" tabindex="-1">lrsi <a class="header-anchor" href="#lrsi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;lrsi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">lrsi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">alpha</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0.2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>RSI Laguerre Filter</strong> is a technical indicator that combines the Relative Strength Index (RSI) with Laguerre filtering techniques. It aims to provide smoother and more responsive signals compared to traditional RSI indicators by applying Laguerre filtering to the RSI values.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>alpha</code>: float - default=0.2</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="ma" tabindex="-1">ma <a class="header-anchor" href="#ma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ma&quot;">​</a></h2><div <strong>Moving Average Adaptive Q</strong> is a technical indicator designed to adapt to changing market conditions by dynamically adjusting the smoothing factor of the moving average. It aims to provide smoother and more accurate trend signals by automatically optimizing the smoothing parameter based on recent price data.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=11</li><li><code>fast_period</code>: int - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="mab" tabindex="-1">mab <a class="header-anchor" href="#mab" aria-label="Permalink to style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, devdn: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, fast_matype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, slow_matype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> MAB</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Moving Average Bands</strong> are a type of technical indicator that consists of multiple moving averages plotted above and below the asset&#39;s price. These bands serve as dynamic support and resistance levels, expanding or contracting based on market volatility. As with <em>ma</em> you can use all available ma types - even different ones for the slow and fast period.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fast_period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>slow_period</code>: int - default=50</li><li><code>devup</code>: float - default=1</li><li><code>devdn</code>: float - default=1</li><li><code>fast_matype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>slow_matype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>MAB(upperband, middleband, lowerband)</p><h2 id="macd" tabindex="-1">macd <a class="header-anchor" href="#macd" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;macd&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">macd(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fast_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">12</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">slow_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">26</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">signal_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">9</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> MACD</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Moving Average Convergence Divergence (MACD)</strong> is a momentum indicator that consists of two lines: the MACD line and the signal line. The MACD line is calculated by subtracting the longer-term Exponential Moving Average (EMA) from the shorter-term EMA. The signal line is a moving average of the MACD line. Traders use the MACD to identify bullish and bearish momentum signals, trend reversals, and divergence between price and momentum.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fast_period</code>: int - default=12</li><li><code>slow_period</code>: int - default=26</li><li><code>signal_period</code>: int - default=9</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>MACD(macd, signal, hist)</p><h2 id="mama" tabindex="-1">mama <a class="header-anchor" href="#mama" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mama&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">mama(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fastlimit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0.5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">slowlimit</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0.05</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> MAMA</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>MESA Adaptive Moving Average (MAMA)</strong> is a technical indicator developed by John F. Ehlers. It utilizes a complex mathematical formula to adaptively adjust the smoothing period of a moving average based on market volatility. MAMA aims to provide smoother and more responsive trend signals compared to traditional moving averages, making it particularly useful for trend-following strategies in dynamic market conditions.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fastlimit</code>: float - default=0.5</li><li><code>slowlimit</code>: float - default=0.05</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>MAMA(mama, fama)</p><h2 id="marketfi" tabindex="-1">marketfi <a class="header-anchor" href="#marketfi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;marketfi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">marketfi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Market Facilitation Index</strong> (MFI) is a volume-based indicator developed by Bill Williams. It measures the ease of price movement based on changes in trading volume. The MFI is calculated by dividing the difference between the high and low prices by the volume. It helps traders identify periods of low liquidity, consolidation, and potential breakout opportunities in the market.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="mass" tabindex="-1">mass <a class="header-anchor" href="#mass" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mass&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">mass(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Mass Index</strong> is a technical indicator developed by Donald Dorsey. It measures the range expansion of prices to identify potential trend reversals. The Mass Index calculates the difference between two exponential moving averages of the high-low range and then applies a smoothing function to create an index.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="mcginley-dynamic" tabindex="-1">mcginley_dynamic <a class="header-anchor" href="#mcginley-dynamic" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mcginley\_dynamic&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">mcginley_dynamic(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">k</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0.6</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>McGinley Dynamic</strong> is a technical indicator developed by John McGinley. It is a moving average designed to track price movements more accurately compared to traditional moving averages. The McGinley Dynamic adjusts its speed based on market conditions, becoming more responsive during volatile periods and smoothing out during quieter times.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>k</code>: float - default=0.6</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="mean-ad" tabindex="-1">mean_ad <a class="header-anchor" href="#mean-ad" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mean\_ad&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">mean_ad(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;hl2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Mean Absolute Deviation</strong> is a statistical measure used to quantify the dispersion of data points around their mean or median. It is calculated by taking the average of the absolute differences between each data point and the mean or median of the dataset. MAD provides insights into the variability or spread of a dataset and is commonly to assess risk and volatility.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;hl2&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="median-ad" tabindex="-1">median_ad <a class="header-anchor" href="#median-ad" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;median\_ad&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">median_ad(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;hl2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Median Absolute Deviation</strong> is a statistical measure used to quantify the dispersion of data points around their median. It is calculated by taking the median of the absolute differences between each data point and the median of the dataset. It is robust to outliers and provides insights into the variability or spread of a dataset, similar to Mean Absolute Deviation, but using the median instead of the mean.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;hl2&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="medprice" tabindex="-1">medprice <a class="header-anchor" href="#medprice" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;medprice&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">medprice(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Median Price (MEDPRICE)</strong> calculates the median of the high and low prices for each period. It provides a single price value that represents the central tendency of the price range over a specified period.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="mfi" tabindex="-1">mfi <a class="header-anchor" href="#mfi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mfi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">mfi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Money Flow Index (MFI)</strong> is a momentum indicator that measures the strength and direction of money flowing in and out of a security. It combines price and volume data to assess buying and selling pressure. The MFI is calculated using a formula that compares typical price changes with volume, generating values between 0 and 100.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="midpoint" tabindex="-1">midpoint <a class="header-anchor" href="#midpoint" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;midpoint&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">midpoint(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>MidPoint</strong> is a technical indicator that calculates the midpoint price of a financial instrument over a specified period. It is calculated by taking the average of the current and the previous candle.</p><p>#filter</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="midprice" tabindex="-1">midprice <a class="header-anchor" href="#midprice" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;midprice&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">midprice(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>MidPrice</strong> is basically just hl2</p><p>#filter</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="minmax" tabindex="-1">minmax <a class="header-anchor" href="#minmax" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;minmax&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">minmax(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">order</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> EXTREMA</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The &quot;<strong>minmax</strong>&quot; function is a mathematical operation that retrieves the extrema (i.e., the minimum and maximum values) from a dataset or a specified range of values. It can be used to identify the lowest and highest values within a given dataset. This operation is often employed to find support and resistance levels in the market.</p><p>#trend</p><p>Also called ZigZag sometimes.</p><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Signal delayed</p><p>Due to the nature of extrema detection signals are always delayed by the amount of order. Meaning you will never get the signal at the time of occurence. This means this is not working for <code>is_min</code> and <code>is_max</code>: <code>[-1]</code>, as this will always be false. Working: <code>[-(order+1)]</code>.</p></div><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>order</code>: int - default = 3</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>EXTREMA(is_min, is_max, last_min, last_max)</p><h2 id="mom" tabindex="-1">mom <a class="header-anchor" href="#mom" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mom&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">mom(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Momentum (MOM)</strong> indicator is used to measure the rate of change in price movements over a specified period. It calculates the difference between the current closing price and the closing price from a previous period. Positive values indicate upward momentum, while negative values indicate downward momentum.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="mwdx" tabindex="-1">mwdx <a class="header-anchor" href="#mwdx" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;mwdx&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light <strong>MWDX Average</strong> is a customized version of the exponential moving average (EMA), providing traders with a smoothed representation of price data with adjustable sensitivity controlled by - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="natr" tabindex="-1">natr <a class="header-anchor" href="#natr" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;natr&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">natr(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Normalized Average True Range (NATR)</strong> is a technical indicator that measures market volatility. It is derived from the Average True Range (ATR) indicator but is normalized to a percentage scale. The NATR calculates the ratio of the current ATR value to the closing price, providing a volatility measure relative to the price level. The NATR is commonly used to assess the magnitude of price movements and to set appropriate stop-loss and take-profit levels.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="nma" tabindex="-1">nma <a class="header-anchor" href="#nma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;nma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">nma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span <strong>Natural Moving Average (NMA)</strong> is a dynamic moving average that adjusts its smoothing factor based on market volatility, providing smoother trend signals in changing market conditions.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=40</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="nvi" tabindex="-1">nvi <a class="header-anchor" href="#nvi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;nvi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">nvi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Negative Volume Index (NVI)</strong> focuses on the relationship between volume and price changes. It is based on the premise that during periods of low volume, smart money investors are more active, and vice versa. The NVI calculates a cumulative index that increases when prices decrease on lower-than-average volume and decreases when prices increase on lower-than-average volume. Traders use the NVI to identify potential distribution phases in the market and to confirm bearish trends.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="obv" tabindex="-1">obv <a class="header-anchor" href="#obv" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;obv&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">obv(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>On Balance Volume (OBV)</strong> is a momentum indicator that uses volume flow to predict changes in stock price. It measures buying and selling pressure by adding the volume on up days and subtracting the volume on down days. The OBV line rises when volume on up days is greater than volume on down days, indicating buying pressure, and falls when the opposite is true, indicating selling pressure.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="pfe" tabindex="-1">pfe <a class="header-anchor" href="#pfe" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;pfe&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">pfe(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, smoothing: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Polarized Fractal Efficiency (PFE)</strong> measures how efficiently price moves over time. It calculates the ratio of actual price movement to the ideal straight-line movement between two points. PFE values range from 0 to 1, where 1 indicates perfect efficiency and 0 suggests inefficiency.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>smoothing</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="pivot" tabindex="-1">pivot <a class="header-anchor" href="#pivot" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;pivot&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">pivot(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">mode</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> PIVOT</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Pivot Points</strong> are a type of technical indicator used to identify potential support and resistance levels in trading. They are calculated using the previous day&#39;s high, low, and close prices. The main pivot point indicates a potential turning point in market sentiment, with other support and resistance levels derived from it. Pivot Points are commonly used to determine entry and exit points.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>mode</code>: int - default = 0</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>PIVOT(r4, r3, r2, r1, pp, s1, s2, s3, s4)</p><div class="tip custom-block"><p class="custom-block-title">Available mode and levels</p><ul><li>0: Standard Pivot Points / Floor Pivot Points - r2, r1, pp, s1, s2</li><li>1: Fibonacci Pivot Points - r3, r2, r1, pp, s1, s2, s3</li><li>2: Demark Pivot Points - r1, pp, s1</li><li>3: Camarilla Pivot Points - r4, r3, r2, r1, pp, s1, s2, s3, s4</li><li>4: Woodie&#39;s Pivot Points - r4, r3, r2, r1, pp, s1, s2, s3, s4</li></ul></div><h2 id="pma" tabindex="-1">pma <a class="header-anchor" href="#pma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;pma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">pma(candles: np.ndarray, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;hl2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> PMA</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Ehlers Predictive Moving Average</strong> is a type of moving average developed by John Ehlers. Unlike traditional moving averages, which rely solely on historical price data, the Predictive Moving Average attempts to predict future price movement by applying a series of calculations based on the current and past prices. It aims to reduce lag and provide more timely signals for traders.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;hl2&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>PMA(predict, trigger)</p><h2 id="ppo" tabindex="-1">ppo <a class="header-anchor" href="#ppo" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ppo&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">ppo(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">fast_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">12</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">slow_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">26</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">matype</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">  float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Percentage Price Oscillator (PPO)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that measures the difference between two moving averages as a percentage of the larger moving average. It helps traders identify bullish and bearish trends in the market. The PPO is calculated by subtracting the longer-term moving average from the shorter-term moving average and then dividing the result by the longer-term moving average.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fast_period</code>: int - default=12</li><li><code>slow_period</code>: int - default=26</li><li><code>matype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="pvi" tabindex="-1">pvi <a class="header-anchor" href="#pvi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;pvi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">pvi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Positive Volume Index (PVI)</strong> is used identify the strength of positive volume flows. It calculates cumulative volume changes based on days when the volume increases from the previous day. The PVI increases when the volume for the current day is greater than the volume for the previous day and decreases when the volume is lower.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="pwma" tabindex="-1">pwma <a class="header-anchor" href="#pwma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;pwma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">pwma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Pascal&#39;s Weighted Moving Average (PWMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that assigns weights to each data point in the series based on Pascal&#39;s triangle. It calculates the weighted average of the data points, giving more importance to recent data while still considering historical data. This weighting scheme aims to provide a smoother representation of the underlying trend compared to simple moving averages. PWMA is particularly useful for traders who prefer a moving average that reacts quickly to recent price changes while reducing noise from erratic price movements.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="qstick" tabindex="-1">qstick <a class="header-anchor" href="#qstick" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;qstick&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">qstick(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Qstick</strong> measures the difference between opening and closing prices over a period, indicating buying (positive values) or selling (negative values) pressure. It helps identify trends and potential reversals, with positive values signaling bullish and negative values bearish trends. Traders watch for deviations from the zero line to spot overbought or oversold conditions.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="reflex" tabindex="-1">reflex <a class="header-anchor" href="#reflex" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;reflex&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">reflex(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">20</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Reflex indicator by John F. Ehlers</strong> aims to filter out high-frequency noise in price data while retaining trend information. It calculates the difference between the current price and the price &#39;n&#39; bars ago, where &#39;n&#39; is a user-defined parameter. This difference is then smoothed using a smoothing function.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=20</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="roc" tabindex="-1">roc <a class="header-anchor" href="#roc" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;roc&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">roc(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Rate of Change (ROC)</strong> indicator measures the percentage change in price from one period to the next. It calculates the difference between the current price and the price &#39;n&#39; periods ago, then expresses this difference as a percentage of the previous price. Mathematically, it is represented as ((price/prevPrice) - 1) * 100.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="rocp" tabindex="-1">rocp <a class="header-anchor" href="#rocp" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rocp&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rocp(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Rate of Change Percentage (ROCP)</strong> indicator, also known as the Price Rate-of-Change, measures the percentage change in price over a specified number of periods. It calculates the percentage difference between the current price and the price &#39;n&#39; periods ago. Mathematically: (price-prevPrice)/prevPrice.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="rocr" tabindex="-1">rocr <a class="header-anchor" href="#rocr" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rocr&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rocr(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Rate of Change Ratio (ROCR)</strong> indicator measures the ratio of the current price to the price &#39;n&#39; periods ago. Mathematically, it is represented as (price / prevPrice).</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="rocr100" tabindex="-1">rocr100 <a class="header-anchor" href="#rocr100" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rocr100&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rocr100(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>ROCR100, or Rate of Change Ratio 100, is a momentum indicator that measures the percentage change in price over a specified period. It calculates the ratio of the current price to the price &#39;n&#39; periods ago and expresses the result as a percentage. (price / prevPrice) * 100</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="roofing" tabindex="-1">roofing <a class="header-anchor" href="#roofing" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;roofing&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">48</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">lp_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span
