Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Roofing Filter</strong> is a technical indicator developed by John F. Ehlers. It&#39;s designed to smooth out market cycles and reduce noise in price data, making it easier to identify trends. The indicator utilizes a bandpass filter to extract the dominant cycle components of the price series. By filtering out the shorter-term and longer-term cycles, the Roofing Filter aims to provide a clearer view of the underlying trend.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>hp_period</code>: int - default=48</li><li><code>lp_period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="rsi" tabindex="-1">rsi <a class="header-anchor" href="#rsi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rsi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rsi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Relative Strength Index (RSI)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that measures the speed and change of price movements. It oscillates between 0 and 100 and is typically used to identify overbought or oversold conditions in an asset. RSI is calculated using the average gain and average loss over a specified period, often 14 periods by default. Traders often look for divergences between RSI and price movements to anticipate potential trend reversals. High RSI values suggest overbought conditions, while low RSI values indicate oversold conditions.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="rsmk" tabindex="-1">rsmk <a class="header-anchor" href="#rsmk" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rsmk&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rsmk(candles: np.ndarray, candles_compare: np.ndarray, lookback: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 90</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, signal_period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 20</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> RSMK</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Relative Strength (RSMK)</strong> indicator measures the ratio of the price of one security to another over a specified period. It calculates the relative strength by taking the logarithm of the ratio of the price of the first security to the price of the second security, and then applies a moving average to smooth the result. This indicator helps identify potential trends or reversals in the performance of one security relative to another.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>lookback</code>: int - default=90</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=3</li><li><code>signal_period</code>: int - default=20</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>RSMK(indicator, signal)</p><h2 id="rsx" tabindex="-1">rsx <a class="header-anchor" href="#rsx" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rsx&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rsx(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>RSX (Relative Strength Xtra)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that helps identify overbought and oversold conditions in the market. It is calculated by applying an exponential smoothing function to the ratio of the average gain to the average loss over a specified period.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="rvi" tabindex="-1">rvi <a class="header-anchor" href="#rvi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;rvi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">rvi(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span 14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, matype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, devtype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Relative Volatility Index (RVI)</strong> measures directional volatility by comparing smoothed moving averages of positive and negative price changes. It calculates the ratio of upward and downward volatility averages using a specified deviation type (standard, mean, or median) and a moving average for smoothing.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>ma_len</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>matype</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>devtype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="safezonestop" tabindex="-1">safezonestop <a class="header-anchor" href="#safezonestop" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;safezonestop&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">safezonestop(candles: np.ndarray, period: 22</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, mult: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 2.5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, max_lookback: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, direction: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;long&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]:</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Safezone Stops</strong> indicator calculates stop levels for long or short positions based on price volatility. For long positions, it computes the maximum between the previous low minus a multiple of the negative directional movement and a specified lookback period. For short positions, it calculates the minimum between the previous high plus a multiple of the positive directional movement and the specified lookback period.</p><p>#exit</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=22</li><li><code>mult</code>: float - default=2.5</li><li><code>max_lookback</code>: int - default=3</li><li><code>direction</code>: str - default=&quot;long&quot; (&quot;short&quot;)</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="sar" tabindex="-1">sar <a class="header-anchor" href="#sar" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;sar&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">sar(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">acceleration</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0.02</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">maximum</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0.2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Parabolic SAR (SAR)</strong> is a trend-following indicator used to identify potential reversal points in price movements. It plots dots above or below the price to indicate trend direction. Parameters like acceleration and maximum values control its sensitivity. Traders use it for entry and exit signals, with dots switching positions suggesting trend reversals.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>acceleration</code>: float - default=0.02</li><li><code>maximum</code>: float - default=0.2</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="sinwma" tabindex="-1">sinwma <a class="header-anchor" href="#sinwma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;sinwma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">sinwma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span 14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Sine Weighted Moving Average (SINWMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that assigns different weights to each data point based on the sine function. This weighting scheme gives more importance to recent data points while gradually reducing the influence of older data points. As a result, the SINWMA is sensitive to changes in trend direction, making it useful for trend-following strategies.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="skew" tabindex="-1">skew <a class="header-anchor" href="#skew" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;skew&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">skew(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;hl2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Skewness</strong> measures the asymmetry of a probability distribution. Positive skewness indicates a right-leaning distribution, negative skewness implies a left-leaning one, and zero skewness means perfect symmetry.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;hl2&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="sma" tabindex="-1">sma <a class="header-anchor" href="#sma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;sma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">sma(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Simple Moving Average (SMA)</strong> calculates the average price of a security over a specified number of periods. It&#39;s a commonly used technical indicator that helps smooth out price data to identify trends.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="smma" tabindex="-1">smma <a class="header-anchor" href="#smma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;smma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">smma(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Smoothed Moving Average (SMMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that assigns less weight to the most recent data points compared to the Simple Moving Average (SMA). It aims to reduce lag and provide a smoother representation of price trends.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><h2 id="sqwma" tabindex="-1">sqwma <a class="header-anchor" href="#sqwma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;sqwma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">sqwma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Square Weighted Moving Average (SQWMA)</strong> is a type of weighted moving average where the weights applied to each data point are squared. This method assigns greater importance to recent data points while still considering older ones, resulting in a smoother and more responsive moving average compared to traditional methods.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="srsi" tabindex="-1">srsi <a class="header-anchor" href="#srsi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;srsi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">srsi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> StochasticRSI</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Stochastic RSI (SRSI)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that combines elements of both the Relative Strength Index (RSI) and the Stochastic Oscillator. It measures the relative position of the RSI within its range over a specified period, typically 14 days, and then applies the Stochastic formula to generate values between 0 and 100. This indicator helps traders identify overbought and oversold conditions more effectively than using RSI alone.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>StochasticRSI(k, d)</p><h2 id="srwma" tabindex="-1">srwma <a class="header-anchor" href="#srwma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;srwma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">srwma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Square Root Weighted Moving Average (SRWMA)</strong> assigns weights to each data point based on the square root of its position in the series. This means that more recent data points are given relatively higher importance compared to older ones, similar to other weighted moving averages. It&#39;s useful for smoothing out price data while placing more emphasis on recent price movements.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="stc" tabindex="-1">stc <a class="header-anchor" href="#stc" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;stc&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">stc(candles: np.ndarray, fast_period: </span><span 23</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, fast_matype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, slow_period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 50</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, slow_matype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span 10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, d_period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Schaff Trend Cycle (STC)</strong> is a technical indicator designed to identify market trends and potential reversals. It combines the concepts of cycle analysis and momentum oscillators to produce signals for both trending and range-bound markets. The STC oscillator fluctuates between 0 and 100, where readings above 25 typically indicate bullish momentum, and readings below 75 suggest bearish momentum. Traders often use crossovers and divergences with price action to generate buy or sell signals.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fast_period</code>: int - default=23</li><li><code>fast_matype</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>slow_period</code>: int - default=50</li><li><code>slow_matype</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>k_period</code>: int - default=10</li><li><code>d_period</code>: int - default=3</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="stiffness" tabindex="-1">stiffness <a class="header-anchor" href="#stiffness" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;stiffness&quot;">​</a></h2><p>The Stiffness Indicator is a technical indicator developed by <a href="https://www.tradingview.com/script/MOw6mUQl-Stiffness-Indicator-DaviddTech" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">daviddtech on tradingview</a>, and it is used to measure the power of a trend. The stiffness is calculated based on the moving average and standard deviation of the price.</p><div class="language-py vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">py</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span stiff_length: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span 3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span data.</li><li><code>ma_length</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 100) - Length of the moving average.</li><li><code>stiff_length</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 60) - Length of the stiffness calculation.</li><li><code>stiff_smooth</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 3) - Smoothing period for the stiffness calculation.</li><li><code>source_type</code>: <code>str</code> (default: &quot;close&quot;) - Source type for the candle (e.g., &quot;open&quot;, &quot;high&quot;, &quot;low&quot;, &quot;close&quot;).</li></ul><p><strong>Return Type</strong>: <code>float</code></p><ul><li><code>stiffness</code>: The stiffness value.</li></ul><h2 id="stddev" tabindex="-1">stddev <a class="header-anchor" href="#stddev" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;stddev&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">stddev(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Standard Deviation (STDDEV)</strong> calculates the dispersion of a set of data points from its mean value. It is often used to assess the risk or volatility of an asset&#39;s price movements over a specific period. Higher standard deviation values indicate greater price volatility, while lower values suggest more stable price action. STDDEV is used to gauge potential price fluctuations and adjust trading strategies accordingly.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>nbdev</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="stoch" tabindex="-1">stoch <a class="header-anchor" href="#stoch" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;stoch&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">stoch(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span Stochastic</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Stochastic Oscillator</strong> is a momentum indicator used to spot overbought and oversold conditions in a market. It comprises two lines: %K and %D. Readings above 80 suggest overbought conditions, signaling a potential downturn, while readings below 20 indicate oversold conditions, signaling a possible upturn.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>Stochastic(k, d)</p><h2 id="stochf" tabindex="-1">stochf <a class="header-anchor" href="#stochf" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;stochf&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">stochf(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> StochasticFast</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Stochastic Fast</strong> indicator calculates the fast %K and %D lines. It measures the current closing price relative to the high-low range over a specified period. The %K line represents the current price in relation to the range, while the %D line is a moving average of the %K line.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fastk_period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>fastd_period</code>: int - default=3</li><li><code>fastd_matype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>StochasticFast(k, d)</p><h2 id="supersmoother" tabindex="-1">supersmoother <a class="header-anchor" href="#supersmoother" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;supersmoother&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">supersmoother(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Super Smoother Filter 2-pole</strong> Butterworth is an indicator introduced by John F. Ehlers. It functions as a smoothing filter designed to eliminate aliasing noise while preserving the phase characteristics of the original signal. This filter employs a 2-pole Butterworth filter to achieve its smoothing effect, resulting in a smoother output compared to traditional moving averages.</p><p>#filter</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="supersmoother-3-pole" tabindex="-1">supersmoother_3_pole <a class="header-anchor" href="#supersmoother-3-pole" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;supersmoother\_3\_pole&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">supersmoother_3_pole(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Super Smoother Filter 3-pole</strong> Butterworth, described by John F. Ehlers, is an advanced smoothing filter designed to reduce noise and preserve the phase of the original signal. It utilizes a 3-pole Butterworth filter to achieve even smoother output. This filter is particularly effective in removing high-frequency noise while retaining the essential features of the underlying data.</p><p>#filter</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="swma" tabindex="-1">swma <a class="header-anchor" href="#swma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;swma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">swma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Symmetric Weighted Moving Average (SWMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that assigns weights symmetrically to data points around the center of the window. Unlike simple moving averages where all data points have equal weight, SWMA gives more weight to the values closer to the center of the window and gradually decreases the weight as the distance from the center increases. This weighting scheme allows SWMA to respond more quickly to recent price changes while still providing smoother results compared to other weighted moving averages.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="supertrend" tabindex="-1">supertrend <a class="header-anchor" href="#supertrend" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;supertrend&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">supertrend(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">10</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">factor</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> SuperTrend</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>SuperTrend</strong> is a trend-following indicator that helps identify the direction of the current trend in the market. It is based on the concept of average true range (ATR) and plots a line above or below the price, indicating bullish or bearish trends, respectively. The SuperTrend line changes its position based on the underlying price movement and volatility, providing traders with potential entry and exit signals.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>factor</code>: int - default=3</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>SuperTrend(trend, changed)</p><h2 id="support-resistance-with-breaks" tabindex="-1">support_resistance_with_breaks <a class="header-anchor" href="#support-resistance-with-breaks" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;support_resistance_with_breaks&quot;">​</a></h2><p>This indicator calculates support and resistance levels with break lines based on the provided candle data. Check it out on <a href="https://www.tradingview.com/script/JDFoWQbL-Support-and-Resistance-Levels-with-Breaks-LuxAlgo" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">Tradingview</a> for more information.</p><p><strong>Credits</strong>: <a href="https://www.tradingview.com/script/JDFoWQbL-Support-and-Resistance-Levels-with-Breaks-LuxAlgo" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">LuxAlgo</a></p><div class="language-py vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">py</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">support_resistance_with_breaks(candles: np.ndarray, left_bars: </span><span 15</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, right_bars: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span vol_threshold: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span SupportResistanceWithBreaks</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Properties</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: <code>np.ndarray</code> - Input candle data.</li><li><code>left_bars</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 15) - Number of left bars for support and resistance calculation.</li><li><code>right_bars</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 15) - Number of right bars for support and resistance calculation.</li><li><code>vol_threshold</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 20) - Volume threshold for break detection.</li></ul><p><strong>Return Type</strong>: <code>SupportResistanceWithBreaks</code> containing six values:</p><ul><li><code>support</code>: The calculated support level.</li><li><code>resistance</code>: The calculated resistance level.</li><li><code>red_break</code>: A boolean indicating a red break (bearish signal).</li><li><code>green_break</code>: A boolean indicating a green break (bullish signal).</li><li><code>bear_wick</code>: A boolean indicating a bearish wick.</li><li><code>bull_wick</code>: A boolean indicating a bullish wick.</li></ul><p>This function can be used to identify potential support and resistance levels, as well as detect breaks and wicks in the price action, which can be useful for developing trading strategies.</p><h2 id="t3" tabindex="-1">t3 <a class="header-anchor" href="#t3" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;t3&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Triple Exponential Moving Average (T3)</strong> is a type of moving average that applies triple exponential smoothing to the price data. It is designed to reduce lag and provide smoother trends compared to traditional moving averages. The T3 incorporates multiple exponential moving averages with different smoothing factors to adapt to changing market conditions more effectively.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>vfactor</code>: float - default=0</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="tema" tabindex="-1">tema <a class="header-anchor" href="#tema" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;tema&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">tema(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">9</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Triple Exponential Moving Average (TEMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that applies triple exponential smoothing to the price data. It aims to reduce lag and to provide smoother trends compared to traditional moving averages by incorporating multiple exponential moving averages with different smoothing factors. TEMA responds more rapidly to price changes while maintaining a smoother trajectory, making it useful for trend-following strategies.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=9</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="trange" tabindex="-1">trange <a class="header-anchor" href="#trange" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;trange&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">trange(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>True Range</strong> is a measure of market volatility, representing the greatest of the following:</p><ol><li>The current high minus the current low.</li><li>The absolute value of the current high minus the previous close.</li><li>The absolute value of the current low minus the previous close.</li></ol><p>It provides insight into the price movement range, capturing potential price gaps and sudden shifts. True Range is often used in the calculation of various technical indicators, such as Average True Range (ATR), to assess market volatility and adjust trading strategies accordingly.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="trendflex" tabindex="-1">trendflex <a class="header-anchor" href="#trendflex" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;trendflex&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">trendflex(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">20</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Trendflex</strong> indicator, developed by John F. Ehlers, aims to identify trend reversals by smoothing price data. It combines cycle extraction and trend extraction components to filter out noise and identify underlying trends, providing clearer signals for traders.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=20</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="trima" tabindex="-1">trima <a class="header-anchor" href="#trima" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;trima&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">trima(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">30</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>TRIMA, or <strong>Triangular Moving Average</strong>, is a type of moving average that places equal weight on prices over a specified time period. It is calculated by taking the average of prices over this period, with the middle prices receiving the most weight.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=30</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="trix" tabindex="-1">trix <a class="header-anchor" href="#trix" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;trix&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">trix(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">18</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>TRIX - 1-day Rate-Of-Change (ROC) of a Triple Smooth EMA is a momentum oscillator that measures the percentage change in a triple-smoothed EMA over a specified time period. It calculates the rate of change of the EMA by comparing the current value to the value 1 day ago, then expresses this change as a percentage.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=18</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="tsf" tabindex="-1">tsf <a class="header-anchor" href="#tsf" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;tsf&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">tsf(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Time Series Forecast (TSF)</strong> indicator predicts future price movements based on past price data. It uses linear regression to estimate the future value of the price based on historical prices. TSF extrapolates the trend of the data points and extends it into the future, providing a projection of where the price may go.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="tsi" tabindex="-1">tsi <a class="header-anchor" href="#tsi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;tsi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">tsi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">long_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">25</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">13</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>True Strength Index (TSI)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that measures price strength relative to volatility. TSI is calculated by taking the difference between two moving averages of price momentum and dividing it by the absolute value of the longer-term moving average of price momentum. Positive TSI values indicate bullish momentum, while negative values suggest bearish momentum.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>long_period</code>: int - default=25</li><li><code>short_period</code>: int - default=13</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="ttm-trend" tabindex="-1">ttm_trend <a class="header-anchor" href="#ttm-trend" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ttm\_trend&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;hl2&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>TTM Trend</strong> indicator identifies the prevailing market trend by analyzing price action. It employs proprietary algorithms to determine whether the market is in a bullish (True) or bearish (False) phase.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;hl2&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>bool | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="ttm-squeeze-ttm-squeeze" tabindex="-1">ttm_squeeze (TTM Squeeze) <a class="header-anchor" href="#ttm-squeeze-ttm-squeeze" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ttm_squeeze (TTM Squeeze)&quot;">​</a></h2><p>TTMSqueeze is a technical indicator that identifies potential squeeze situations in the market. It combines Bollinger Bands and Keltner Channels to detect when the volatility is decreasing, indicating a potential breakout.</p><p><strong>Author:</strong> daviddtech</p><p><strong>Credits:</strong> <a href="https://www.tradingview.com/script/Mh3EmxF5-TTM-Squeeze-DaviddTech/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">https://www.tradingview.com/script/Mh3EmxF5-TTM-Squeeze-DaviddTech/</a></p><h3 id="parameters" tabindex="-1">Parameters <a class="header-anchor" href="#parameters" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Parameters&quot;">​</a></h3><div class="language-py vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">py</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">ttm_squeeze(candles: np.ndarray, length_ttms: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span bb_mult_ttms: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 2.0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, kc_mult_low_ttms: </span><span
