bool</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Properties</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: <code>np.ndarray</code> - Input candle data.</li><li><code>length_ttms</code>: <code>int</code> (default: 20) - Period for the Bollinger Bands and Keltner Channels.</li><li><code>bb_mult_ttms</code>: <code>float</code> (default: 2.0) - Multiplier for the Bollinger Bands.</li><li><code>kc_mult_low_ttms</code>: <code>float</code> (default: 2.0) - Multiplier for the lower Keltner Channel.</li></ul><p><strong>Return Type</strong>: <code>bool</code></p><p><strong>Return Value</strong>: <code>True</code> if a squeeze situation is detected, <code>False</code> otherwise.</p><p>This indicator is useful for identifying potential breakout situations in the market. It can be used in conjunction with other indicators to form a comprehensive trading strategy.</p><h2 id="typprice" tabindex="-1">typprice <a class="header-anchor" href="#typprice" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;typprice&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">typprice(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Typical Price (TYPPRICE)</strong> represents the average price of a security over a specific period. It&#39;s calculated by adding the high, low, and closing prices of a candle and then dividing the sum by three. This indicator is useful for smoothing out price fluctuations and providing a clearer picture of the underlying trend.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="ui" tabindex="-1">ui <a class="header-anchor" href="#ui" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ui&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">ui(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, scalar: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">,  sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Ulcer Index (UI)</strong> is a technical indicator designed to measure the downside volatility of an investment. It helps investors and traders assess the risk associated with a particular investment by quantifying the extent and duration of drawdowns or declines from previous peaks. The Ulcer Index is calculated by taking the square root of the mean of the squared percentage drawdowns over a specified period, usually 14 days. A higher Ulcer Index value indicates higher volatility and greater risk.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>scalar</code>: float - default=100</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="ultosc" tabindex="-1">ultosc <a class="header-anchor" href="#ultosc" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;ultosc&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">ultosc(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">timeperiod1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">7</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">timeperiod2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">timeperiod3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">28</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">  float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Ultimate Oscillator (ULTOSC)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that blends short-term, intermediate-term, and long-term price action into one indicator. It ranges between 0 and 100, helping traders spot overbought and oversold conditions and potential trend reversals.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>timeperiod1</code>: int - default=7</li><li><code>timeperiod2</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>timeperiod3</code>: int - default=28</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="var" tabindex="-1">var <a class="header-anchor" href="#var" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;var&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">var(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Variance</strong> is a statistical measure that quantifies the degree of dispersion or spread in a dataset. It calculates the average of the squared differences from the mean. In finance, variance is often used to assess the volatility or risk of an asset&#39;s returns.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>nbdev</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vi" tabindex="-1">vi <a class="header-anchor" href="#vi" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vi&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">vi(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> VI</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Vortex Indicator (VI)</strong> is a technical analysis tool that consists of two components: the Positive Vortex Indicator (+VI) and the Negative Vortex Indicator (-VI). These components are represented by the named tuple VI, which includes the values for both the positive and negative indicators.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>VI(plus, minus)</p><h2 id="vidya" tabindex="-1">vidya <a class="header-anchor" href="#vidya" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vidya&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">vidya(candles: np.ndarray, length: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Variable Index Dynamic Average (VIDYA)</strong> is a type of moving average that dynamically adjusts its sensitivity based on market volatility. It aims to provide smoother and more responsive results compared to traditional moving averages. VIDYA is calculated using a variable index factor that adapts to changing market conditions, making it suitable for trend-following strategies.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>length</code>: int - default=9</li><li><code>fix_cmo</code>: bool - default=True</li><li><code>select</code>: bool - default=True</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vpci" tabindex="-1">vpci <a class="header-anchor" href="#vpci" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vpci&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">vpci(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">short_range</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">long_range</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">25</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> VPCI</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Volume Price Confirmation Indicator (VPCI)</strong> is a technical analysis tool used to confirm price movements based on volume. It combines both price and volume data to assess the strength of a trend. VPCI compares the percentage change in price to the percentage change in volume over a specified period. By analyzing the relationship between price and volume, traders can gain insights into the sustainability of price movements and potential trend reversals.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>short_range</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>long_range</code>: int - default=25</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>VPCI(vpci, vpcis)</p><h2 id="vlma" tabindex="-1">vlma <a class="header-anchor" href="#vlma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vlma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Variable Length Moving Average (VLMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that adjusts its length based on market conditions. Unlike traditional moving averages with fixed periods, the VLMA dynamically changes its period length in response to changes in volatility or other predefined criteria. This adaptive nature allows the VLMA to better capture shifts in the underlying price trend, potentially providing more timely and accurate signals to traders.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>min_period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>max_period</code>: int - default=50</li><li><code>matype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>devtype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vosc" tabindex="-1">vosc <a class="header-anchor" href="#vosc" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vosc&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">vosc(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">short_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">2</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">long_period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Volume Oscillator (VOSC)</strong> is a momentum oscillator that measures the difference between two volume-based moving averages. It helps traders identify bullish and bearish trends in trading volume. The VOSC is calculated by subtracting a longer-term volume moving average from a shorter-term volume moving average. This difference is then plotted as a histogram or a line chart, providing insights into the strength and direction of volume trends.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>short_period</code>: int - default=2</li><li><code>long_period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="voss" tabindex="-1">voss <a class="header-anchor" href="#voss" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;voss&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki VossFilter</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Voss Filter</strong> indicator by John Ehlers tries to identify price patterns and predict future price movements. It applies filters to smooth the price data and extract relevant signals.</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=20</li><li><code>predict</code>: int - It&#39;s calculated by cumulatively adding the percentage change in price multiplied by volume over a specified period.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vpwma" tabindex="-1">vpwma <a class="header-anchor" href="#vpwma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vpwma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">vpwma(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, power: &quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Variable Power Weighted Moving Average (VPWMA)</strong> adjusts the weights of each price data point in its calculation based on their respective volumes. This means that periods with higher trading volumes have a greater influence on the moving average.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>power</code>: float - default=0.382</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vwap" tabindex="-1">vwap <a class="header-anchor" href="#vwap" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;vwap&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span <strong>Volume Weighted Average Price (VWAP)</strong> calculates the average price of a financial asset over a specified time period, weighted by the trading volume during each period. It provides insight into the average price at which a security has traded throughout the day, based on both volume and price. The <code>anchor</code> parameter allows you to specify the time interval for which the VWAP is calculated.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>anchor</code>: str - ‘D‘ - (‘Y’), months (‘M’), weeks (‘W’), days (‘D’), hours (‘h’), minutes (‘m’)</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vwma" tabindex="-1">vwma <a class="header-anchor" href="#vwma" <strong>Volume Weighted Moving Average (VWMA)</strong> is a type of moving average that considers the volume traded at each price level. It calculates the average price of a financial asset over a specified time period, with each price point weighted by its corresponding trading volume. This provides a more accurate representation of average price levels compared to traditional moving averages.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="vwmacd" tabindex="-1">vwmacd <a class="header-anchor" href="#vwmacd" aria-label="Permalink to volume-weighted moving averages. It is primarily used to identify changes in momentum based on both price and volume data.</p><p><strong>Author:</strong> David.</p><p><strong>Credits:</strong> <a href="https://www.tradingview.com/script/33Y1LzRq-Volume-Weighted-Moving-Average-Convergence-Divergence-MACD/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">https://www.tradingview.com/script/33Y1LzRq-Volume-Weighted-Moving-Average-Convergence-Divergence-MACD/</a></p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>fast_period</code>: int - It helps traders identify potential reversals or confirm trends by analyzing the relationship between price and volume.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="waddah-attar-explosion" tabindex="-1">Waddah Attar Explosion <a class="header-anchor" href="#waddah-attar-explosion" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;Waddah Attar Explosion&quot;">​</a></h2><p>The Addah Attar Explosion is a technical indicator that combines the Moving Average Convergence Divergence (MACD) with Bollinger Bands to identify potential trend reversals and explosions in price action. This indicator to LazyBear and available onView.</p><p>#trend</p><h3 id="parameters-1" tabindex="-1">Parameters <a class="header-anchor" href="#parameters-1" aria-label="Permalink to value.</li><li><code>trend</code>: The trend direction value (1 for upward trend, -1 for downward trend).</li></ul><p>This indicator is useful for identifying potential trend reversals and explosions in price action, and can be used in conjunction with other indicators to form a comprehensive trading strategy.</p><h2 id="wclprice" tabindex="-1">wclprice <a class="header-anchor" href="#wclprice" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;wclprice&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">wclprice(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Weighted Close Price (WCLPRICE)</strong> is a technical indicator that calculates the average of high, low, and twice the closing price. It provides a weighted representation of the closing price and is often used in technical analysis to identify trends and potential reversal points in the market.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="wilders" tabindex="-1">wilders <a class="header-anchor" href="#wilders" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;wilders&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">wilders(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">5</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Wilders Smoothing</strong>, named after its creator J. Welles Wilder Jr., is a method used to smooth time series data, such as prices or indicators. It applies an exponential moving average (EMA) with a smoothing factor of 1/n, where n is the period specified. This smoothing technique assigns more weight to recent data points, making it responsive to current market conditions.</p><p>#filter</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=5</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="willr" tabindex="-1">willr <a class="header-anchor" href="#willr" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;willr&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">willr(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p><strong>Williams&#39; %R</strong>, developed by Larry Williams, is a momentum indicator that measures overbought or oversold conditions in a financial instrument. It is calculated as the difference between the highest high of the specified period and the current closing price, divided by the highest high minus the lowest low of the period, multiplied by -100. The result oscillates between -100 and 0, where values above -20 indicate overbought conditions, and values below -80 indicate oversold conditions.</p><p>#momentum</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="wma" tabindex="-1">wma <a class="header-anchor" href="#wma" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;wma&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">wma(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">30</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Weighted Moving Average (WMA)</strong> is a technical analysis indicator that calculates the average price of a security over a specified time period, giving more weight to recent data points. Unlike simple moving averages, which assign equal weight to each data point, WMAs assign greater weight to more recent prices. This is achieved by multiplying each price by a weighting factor determined by its position in the data series. The WMA is used to identify trends and smooth out price fluctuations over time.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=30</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="wt" tabindex="-1">wt <a class="header-anchor" href="#wt" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;wt&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">wt(candles: np.ndarray, wtchannellen: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 9</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, wtaveragelen: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 12</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, wtmalen: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, oblevel: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 53</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">,  oslevel: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> -</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">53</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, source_type: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">str</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;"> &quot;hlc3&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Wavetrend</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Wavetrend</strong> indicator combines moving averages to identify trend strength and direction. It offers buy signals when the trend line crosses above the signal line, indicating a bullish trend, and sell signals when it crosses below, suggesting a bearish trend.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>wtchannellen</code>: int - period=9</li><li><code>wtaveragelen</code>: int - period=12</li><li><code>wtmalen</code>: int - period=3</li><li><code>oblevel</code>: int - period=53</li><li><code>oslevel</code>: int - period=-53</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - period=&quot;hlc3&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - period=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>Wavetrend(wt1, wt2, wtCrossUp, wtCrossDown, wtOversold, wtOverbought, wtVwap)</p><h2 id="zlema" tabindex="-1">zlema <a class="header-anchor" href="#zlema" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;zlema&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">zlema(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">20</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Zero-Lag Exponential Moving Average (ZLEMA)</strong> is designed to reduce lag associated with traditional exponential moving averages. It achieves this by using a subtraction factor to eliminate delay, resulting in a smoother and more responsive moving average.</p><p>#trend</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=20</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="zscore" tabindex="-1">zscore <a class="header-anchor" href="#zscore" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;zscore&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">zscore(candles: np.ndarray, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">period</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">14</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">matype</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">nbdev</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">1</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, devtype: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">source_type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF;">&quot;close&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">sequential</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Union[</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;">  float</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, np.ndarray]</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>zScore</strong> indicator measures the distance between a data point and the mean of a dataset in terms of standard deviations. It helps identify overbought and oversold conditions based on how far the current value deviates from the mean.</p><p>#volatility</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=14</li><li><code>matype</code>: int - default=0</li><li><code>nbdev</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>devtype</code>: int - default=1</li><li><code>source_type</code>: str - default=&quot;close&quot;</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>float | np.ndarray</p><h2 id="volume" tabindex="-1">volume <a class="header-anchor" href="#volume" aria-label="Permalink to &quot;volume&quot;">​</a></h2><div class="language-python vp-adaptive-theme"><button title="Copy Code" class="copy"></button><span class="lang">python</span><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark vp-code" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">volume(candles: np.ndarray, period: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">int</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> 20</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">, sequential: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70;">bool</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583;"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF;"> False</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#B31D28;--shiki-light-font-style:italic;--shiki-dark:#FDAEB7;--shiki-dark-font-style:italic;">-&gt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8;"> Volume</span></span></code></pre></div><p>The <strong>Volume</strong> indicator returns the volume of the current candle and its moving average.</p><p><strong>Arguments</strong>:</p><ul><li><code>candles</code>: np.ndarray</li><li><code>period</code>: int - default=20</li><li><code>sequential</code>: bool - default=False</li></ul><p><strong>Returns</strong>:</p><p>Volume(volume, ma)</p></div></div></main><footer class="VPDocFooter" data-v-39a288b8 data-v-e257564d><!--[--><!--]--><div class="edit-info" data-v-e257564d><div class="edit-link" data-v-e257564d><a class="VPLink link vp-external-link-icon no-icon edit-link-button" href="https://github.com/jesse-ai/docs/edit/master/docs/docs/indicators/reference.md" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" data-v-e257564d><!--[--><span class="vpi-square-pen edit-link-icon" data-v-e257564d></span> Edit this page on GitHub<!--]--></a></div><!----></div><nav class="prev-next" aria-labelledby="doc-footer-aria-label" data-v-e257564d><span class="visually-hidden" id="doc-footer-aria-label" data-v-e257564d>Pager</span><div class="pager" data-v-e257564d><a class="VPLink link pager-link prev" href="/docs/indicators/" data-v-e257564d><!--[--><span class="desc" data-v-e257564d>Previous page</span><span class="title" data-v-e257564d>Introduction</span><!--]--></a></div><div class="pager" data-v-e257564d><a class="VPLink link pager-link next" href="/docs/indicators/custom-indicators" data-v-e257564d><!--[--><span class="desc" data-v-e257564d>Next page</span><span class="title" data-v-e257564d>Custom Indicators</span><!--]--></a></div></nav></footer><!--[--><!--]--></div></div></div><!--[--><!--]--></div></div><footer class="VPFooter has-sidebar" data-v-5d98c3a5 data-v-e315a0ad><div class="container" data-v-e315a0ad><p class="message" data-v-e315a0ad>We do NOT guarantee profitable trading results in anyways.
